class="anchor anchorWithStickyNavbar_loeA" id="3.334">Self-hosted Retool 3.334<a href="#3.334" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Self-hosted Retool 3.334" title="Direct link to Self-hosted Retool 3.334">​</a></h2><p><span class="badge badge--success margin-right--sm">Latest release</span><span class="badge badge--success">Currently supported</span></p><table -->0<!-- -->-stable on Dockerhub</a></td></tr></tbody></table><h3>Major changes in this release</h3><ul><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/multi-instance-releases-ga" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Multi-instance releases for Source Control are now generally available.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/multiplayer-license_key" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">LICENSE_KEY is required for multiplayer on self-hosted starting in Q3 2026.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/a2a" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Agents now support the A2A protocol.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/assist-modes" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Ask and Build mode is now available with Assist.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/assist-thread-summarization" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Assist thread summarization is now available.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/assist-sql" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Improvements to writing SQL with Assist are now available.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/secrets-manager-multiple-configurations" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Multiple Secrets Manager configurations are now available in public beta.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/resource-type-restrictions" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Resource type restrictions are now available for self-hosted Retool.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/assist-layout-editing" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Improvements to editing with Assist are now available.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/workflows-readme" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">README files can now be created for workflows.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/google-slides" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">The Google Slides integration is now available.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/assist-azure" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Assist now supports Azure OpenAI.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/assist-rbac" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Admins can now configure role-based access controls for Assist.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/assist-theming" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Assist now supports additional controls for configuring app themes.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/microsoft-sql" target="_blank" rel="noopener can now be unpublished.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/gpt-5.1" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">OpenAI GPT-5.1 is now available in Retool.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/gpt-5.2" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">OpenAI GPT-5.2 is now available in Retool.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/gemini-3-pro-preview" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Google Gemini 3 Pro Preview is now available in Retool.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/deepseek-models" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">DeepSeek-V3.2 is now supported in Baseten, replacing the deprecated DeepSeek-R1.</a></li></ul><h3>Patch release notes</h3><div><h4 class="anchor anchorWithStickyNavbar_loeA" id="stable-3.334-0">3.334.0 – <!-- --> <!-- -->Mar 3, 2026<a href="#stable-3.334-0" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to stable-3.334-0" title="Direct link to stable-3.334-0">​</a></h4><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>added</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Added support for <code>excludedAttributes=members</code> query parameter in SCIM <code>Get Group</code> API to improve compatibility with SSO providers like Entra ID.</li><li>Added Assignment tab to group pages for RBAC management.</li><li>Enabled the Tavily resource type for all eligible customers.</li><li>Added support for YAML format OpenAPI specifications in OpenAPI resources.</li><li>Added ca-west-1 as a region option for AWS resources.</li><li>Added authorization code grant with PKCE as an OAuth 2.0 option for Snowflake resources.</li><li>Added an accessible focus state for Image components with a click handler.</li><li>Added a <code>folder_id</code> field to public API endpoints for <code>GET /resources</code> and <code>GET /resources/:resourceId</code>.</li><li>Added support for OpenAPI ParameterGroup editor for editing JSON objects in Guided REST mode.</li><li>Added support for returning a list of groups when requested from the <code>GET /user_invites</code> endpoint.</li><li>Added an Assist section to the list of keyboard shortcuts, and added two new shortcuts: <code>Switch to Ask mode</code> and <code>Switch to Build mode</code>.</li><li>Added optional pagination to GET /accessTokens.</li><li>Added optional pagination to GET /user_requests.</li><li>Added a new GET /deployments API endpoint to list source control deployments. Adds additional response body fields to the existing get deployment and trigger deployment endpoints.</li><li>Added support for a <strong>Trigger authentication on every query</strong> option for GraphQL resources.</li><li>Added a list of groups the user is in to the GET /user API endpoint.</li><li>Added the ability for Assist to reference URL parameters when writing queries, transformers, and embedded expressions.</li><li>Fixed an issue in the SCIM API that prevented modification of default groups.</li><li>Added support for additional permissions on business plans.</li><li>Added client credentials authentication for Databricks.</li><li>Added search bar to <strong>Roles &amp; Permissions</strong> page.</li><li>Added a new native video component for mobile apps.</li><li>Added new Secrets Manager scoped secrets behavior: if the <code>SCOPED_SECRETS</code> environment variable is true, then secrets whose names begin with <code>scoped--resources--$FOLDER_NAME--</code> can only be used in resources within the specified folder.</li><li>Added support for pagination on the public API GET /groups method.</li><li>Added support for pagination on the public API GET /folders method.</li><li>Added support for pagination on the public API GET /spaces method.</li><li>Added support for pagination on the public API GET /apps method.</li><li>Added bearer token authentication to MCP resources for use in Agents.</li><li>Added the ability to add and revoke screen access for groups with the API.</li><li>Added support for encoding user email in the Intercom JWT payload for improved authentication.</li><li>Added optional pagination to GET /user_invites for the public API.</li><li>Added optional pagination to GET /environments for the public API.</li><li>Added support for Assist to create forms outside of modals, when the form is the primary purpose of a page.</li><li>Adds a shadow style property and basic organization-level theming support for Alert v2.</li><li>Added spell check support to editable string cells in Table and Key Value components.</li><li>Added support for GPT-5.1.</li><li>Added a shadow style property to the Image component.</li><li>Added <code>initialDeeplink</code> object to the Retool mobile app model for accessing URL parameters and screen navigation information when an app is opened via a deep link.</li><li>Added the <code>ariaLabel</code> property to Link components.</li><li>Added availability for editing &quot;Roles and permissions&quot; to the Business plan.</li><li>Added a shadow style property to the ImageGrid component.</li><li>Added the <code>gemini-3-pro-preview</code> model for use in Retool AI.</li><li>Added an additional permissions banner to the <strong>Groups</strong> page.</li><li>Added support for creating release artifacts of protected workflows from the configured default branch.</li><li>Added a search option to the <strong>Groups</strong> page.</li><li>Adds a notification banner to Assist chat threads for token consumption awareness.</li><li>Added <code>RESOURCE_TYPES_DENY_LIST_CREATE_ONLY</code> env-var, which prevents users from creating new resources of specific types, but does not block queries the way <code>RESOURCE_TYPES_DENY_LIST</code> does.</li><li>Added the <strong>trigger</strong> type to <strong>workflowContext</strong>.</li><li>Added permission guards for resource access via Assist.</li><li>Added sorting options to list of spaces in the <strong>Spaces</strong> settings. Defaults to alphabetical sorting based on space names.</li><li>Added support for Google Slides resources.</li><li>Added support for <code>isEditorMode</code> to <code>QUERY_RUN</code> audit trail log events.</li><li>Added Google Slides tools to Retool Agents.</li><li>Added support for Azure OpenAI as a single model provider for Assist.</li><li>Added support for Google Search grounding in Gemini for Retool AI. You can enable this option in the organizaton&#x27;s <strong>Beta</strong> settings.</li><li>Added the <code>RESOURCE_TYPES_DENY_LIST</code> environment variable to prevent users from creating and running against the provided resource types.</li></ul></div></div></details><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>fixed</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Fixed AWS knowledge base vector queries failing with &quot;AWS region is missing&quot; error.</li><li>Fixed an issue in Signature component when global orientation was not set as default.</li><li>Fixed issue in Query Library where users were unable to add a new resource from the resource picker.</li><li>Fixed navigation to shortlinked apps in presentation mode loading incorrect cached app.</li><li>Fixed drag-and-drop issue with top folder drop zone.</li><li>Fixed folder order when changing scope during drag operations.</li><li>Fixed edit modal from resource dropdown appearing behind workflow canvas.</li><li>Fixed transaction handling in workflow template conversion.</li><li>Fixed <strong>Save</strong> button not appearing when adding or removing members from groups as admin or group admin.</li><li>Improved error message when attempting to rename protected apps.</li><li>Fixed missing environment variable for Java database connector.</li><li>Fixed a bug that caused Secrets Manager secrets in resources not to work in public apps without a logged-in user.</li><li>Fixed mobile video aspect ratio to be dynamic based on the source video dimensions.</li><li>Fixed Scanner component to no longer add an extra leading zero when scanning UPC-A barcodes.</li><li>Fixed an issue that prevented the camera from switching between front and back when using the WebView component in Retool Mobile.</li><li>Fixed layout issue for HTML elements with data-click-target attribute.</li><li>Fixed an issue where the module input window displays a JavaScript error under certain conditions.</li><li>Fixed an issue that caused an error when connecting to Snowflake via OAuth. Retool no longer sends the parameter <code>prompt</code>. This extension to the OAuth protocol is not supported by Snowflake, and was ignored in the past, but now Snowflake treats it as an error.</li><li>Fixed custom groups being unarchived on plan upgrade.</li><li>Fixed an issue where offline jobs would incorrectly parse request bodies as JSON when using non-JSON content types.</li><li>Fixed an issue where workflows libraries <code>requirements.txt</code> showed deleted library.</li><li>Fixed an issue where the <strong>Re-auth</strong> button did not show for resource query tools in the agents tool creation canvas.</li><li>Fixed an issue in workflows where function parameters were not evaluated for a duplicated function.</li><li>Fixed an issue where granted permissions per resource for query authoring were not applied to auto-fixing queries.</li><li>Fixed an issue with string interpolation in OpenAPI query blocks in workflows.</li><li>Fixed an issue where long JavaScript query blocks in workflows caused a bug with scrolling.</li><li>Fixed an issue where Assist users saw an error when using Ask mode and generating apps from scratch with no resources configured in their organization.</li><li>Fixed an issue with the UI in the event handler editor.</li><li>Fixed an issue where users needed to be admins to have access to source control. Users just need manage access.</li><li>Fixed an issue that could cause the OAuth callback URL to be incorrect when using <strong>Share credentials between users</strong> for a resource.</li><li>Fixed an issue with Chart rendering when nested in Stacks.</li><li>Fixed autocomplete in resource fields to not show &quot;secrets&quot; as a global object if Secrets Manager is not enabled.</li><li>Fixed an issue with merging branches in multiplayer.</li><li>Fixed an issue where containers on Android devices get a vertical empty space.</li><li>Fixed an issue that allowed permission group creation on Free and Team plans.</li><li>Fixed unsandboxed execution, which now reads max CPU/memory limits exclusively from env vars.</li><li>Fixed <code>baseDomain</code> shown in source control deployment email alerts.</li><li>Fixed a visual bug in column text colors.</li><li>Fixed an issue so that when the <code>SCOPED_SECRETS</code> env var is enabled, autocompletion for template strings in resources will filter the secrets to omit any scoped secrets that are not available for that resource.</li><li>Fixed an issue where reset password confirmation emails would still be sent to users even when reset password emails are disabled in an organization.</li><li>Fixed an issue where Assist would incorrectly think it could not perform some tasks.</li><li>Fixed an issue with HTML sanitization in the &quot;Failed workflow&quot; alert emails.</li><li>Custom component edits in apps will sync more consistently for multiple editors.</li><li>Fixed an issue where queries containing the word &quot;select&quot; may return an error.</li><li>Fixed an issue with the <strong>State</strong> tab.</li><li>Fixed an issue with scrolling in the <strong>Roles</strong> page.</li><li>Fixed an issue where Assist may remove existing column configuration properties that it doesn&#x27;t support whenever it edits any table column.</li><li>Fixed an issue where the navigation header may flash during redirect.</li><li>Fixed an issue with multi-instance releases so users can protect an element, create a release artifact, and update the manifest in the same PR.</li><li>Fixed an issue where an agent may attempt to continue, before a child agent, invoked as a tool, has finished.</li><li>Fixed an issue where the Source Control branch menu may not load correctly.</li><li>Fixed an issue where Code Executor does not support the <code>LOG_LEVEL</code> environment variable.</li><li>Fixed an issue that prevented the Retool API from creating folders without passing in <code>parent_folder_id</code>.</li><li>Fixes UI issue for thinking box states.</li><li>Fixed non-admin users ability to see the <strong>External Users</strong> group and any groups they are an admin of in <strong>Settings</strong> if they are group admins and have external Retool manage scope.</li><li>Fixed an issue with Retool header flashing on redirect to a workspace.</li><li>Fixed an issue with REST API resources where the <code>metadata.request</code> properties may not always be correctly sanitized.</li><li>Fixed an issue with OpenAPI resources where the <code>metadata.request</code> properties may not always be correctly sanitized.</li><li>Fixed an issue with GraphQL resources where the <code>metadata.request</code> properties may not always be correctly sanitized.</li><li>Fixed issues where Assist failed to add components to header frames.</li><li>Fix an incorrect documentation link for the <strong>Event List</strong> component.</li><li>Fixed an issue when opening an app in the IDE using the <code>historyOffset</code> URL parameter.</li><li>Fixed an issue with placeholders in the <strong>Key Value</strong> component.</li><li>Fixed an issue where tooltips may not appear in the App IDE code editor.</li><li>Fixed an issue with renaming modules.</li><li>Fixed an issue where global error handlers for workflows would trigger even when errors were already handled by block-level <strong>On Error</strong> handlers.</li><li>Fixed dropdown selection issues in the function canvas.</li><li>Fixed token consumption calculation for Assist thread summarization and enabled it by default.</li><li>Fixed a permission check that incorrectly restricted role-based access.</li><li>Fixed an issue where AI queries were not emitting token usage telemetry.</li><li>Fixed an issue where branch syncing incorrectly deleted release artifacts, manifests, and other non-branching files during merge commits.</li><li>Fixed an issue where Azure Repos source control diffs included directory entries as files, which caused deployment errors during partial deploys.</li><li>Fixed an issue where self-hosted instances were incorrectly logging to Retool&#x27;s error tracking service.</li><li>Fixed an issue with GitHub OAuth for MCP resources by including the required <code>Accept: application/json</code> header in access token requests.</li><li>Fixed an issue where admins were unable to delete or move workflows when <code>VERSION_CONTROL_LOCKED</code> is enabled.</li><li>Fixed Assist context window showing incorrect token counts when Anthropic prompt caching is active.</li><li>Fixed source control manifest UI incorrectly passing file paths to Bitbucket API, which caused manifest contents to be wiped.</li><li>Fixed an infinite retry loop in Assist single-shot agent mode.</li><li>Fixed an issue where GitLab source control commits failed due to incorrect encoding of commit actions.</li><li>Fixed template substitution not being applied to form data keys.</li><li>Fixed Assist role-based access controls to correctly apply to the All Users group.</li><li>Fixed an issue where queries using permissioned resources could not be disabled.</li><li>Fixed missing telemetry for AI thread summarization.</li></ul></div></div></details><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" Fixed an issue where very large PDFs in Mobile could cause memory issues. Improved page navigation in the PDF viewer component in Mobile to use native page navigation methods for more reliable page transitions.</li><li>Improved accessibility when setting up two-factor authentication.</li><li>Improved the way that Assist troubleshoots issues.</li><li>Improved UI of the OpenAPI resource editor.</li><li>Improved Assist&#x27;s understanding of how to use the tools available to it.</li><li>Exposed font names in the Theme object.</li><li>Improved the performance of Assist-generated UI changes to large apps.</li><li>Improved Assist&#x27;s ability to write event handler scripts.</li><li>Improved accuracy of custom component library dev modes.</li><li>Adds pagination parameters to the <code>getUsers</code> Retool API endpoint.</li><li>Improved component icon handling for Assist.</li><li>Improved the speed and quality of Assist edits on existing UI layouts.</li><li>Improved the hint when there&#x27;s existing messages in the thread in the Assist input text box.</li><li></li><li>Assist can now verify the configuration of AI models and display an error if verification fails.</li><li>Improved the layout of the <strong>Workflows</strong> tab.</li><li>Improved visibility of errors when protected apps reference unprotected modules.</li><li>Improved error reporting within single-model providers to show model-specific information.</li><li></li><li>Improved workflow execution performance by using compressed block result sizes when determining whether to truncate large results exceeding 10MB.</li><li>Improved the workflow block result omission UI to show users their run logs.</li></ul></div></div></details><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>changed</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Changed terminology from &quot;private beta&quot; to &quot;closed beta&quot; in API endpoints.</li><li>Changed Snowflake Node SDK to use version 2.2.0.</li><li>Changed behavior for Assist to show a loading spinner when Assist is about to execute an auto-submitted prompt.</li><li>Changed Assist behavior so that when the default models are selected, Retool attempts to use the Anthropic resource for Anthropic requests, and sends requests to Anthropic through Amazon Bedrock as a fallback.</li><li>Changed protected trigger feature to be generally available.</li><li>Changed behavior so that if the <code>SCOPED_SECRETS</code> env var is set, secrets with scoped names are shown separately in the Secrets Manager list.</li><li>Renamed the OpenAI resource to OpenAI Platform.</li><li>Updated the app <strong>Share</strong> modal.</li><li>Changed the <strong>Login</strong> Retool Event to be enabled by default.</li><li>Changed references of <strong>AWS Bedrock</strong> to <strong>Amazon Bedrock</strong>.</li><li>User profile pictures now appear when viewing group members.</li><li>Changed required permission level for folder delete, rename, and move to trash operations from <code>edit</code> to <code>own</code> access.</li></ul></div></div></details><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>removed</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Removed the &#x27;Require is not defined&#x27; lint warning in JavaScript code editor.</li><li>Removed OAuth access tokens and non-sensitive ID tokens from audit logs.</li><li>Removed resizability of the <strong>Description</strong> field of a role if the description itself cannot be edited.</li><li>Removed sensitive user tokens from audit logs with OAuth2 SSO.</li><li>Removed user access to app modules in other app pages if they only have access to a specific page, not the entire app.</li><li>Removed expiry warning banners during signup and guided-tour.</li></ul></div></div></details><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>security-fix</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Fixed XSS vulnerability in REST API custom authentication by adding validation for custom auth URLs.</li><li>Upgraded jsPDF library to version 4.0.0 to address CVE-2025-68428.</li><li>Changed behavior so that the HTTP path field in the Databricks resource now sanitizes semicolons to prevent JDBC parameter injection. If you were previously including connection parameters in the HTTP path (e.g., <code>/sql/1.0/warehouses/abc;parameter=value</code>), these will now be stripped. Use the dedicated connection parameters field instead.</li><li>Patched a security issue related to auto-join domains.</li><li>Fixed authorization bypass vulnerability in folder deletion that allowed users without proper permissions to delete folders.</li></ul></div></div></details></div></section><section class="margin-vert--lg"><h2 class="anchor anchorWithStickyNavbar_loeA" future release.</a></li></ul><h3>Patch release notes</h3><div><h4 class="anchor anchorWithStickyNavbar_loeA" id="stable-3.300-15">3.300.15 – <!-- --> <!-- -->Feb 25, 2026<a href="#stable-3.300-15" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to stable-3.300-15" title="Direct link to stable-3.300-15">​</a></h4><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>changed</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Changed required permission level for folder delete, rename, and move to trash operations from <code>edit</code> to <code>own</code> access.</li></ul></div></div></details><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>security-fix</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Fixed authorization bypass vulnerability in folder deletion that allowed users without proper permissions to delete folders.</li></ul></div></div></details></div><div><h4 class="anchor anchorWithStickyNavbar_loeA" id="stable-3.300-14">3.300.14 – <!-- --> <!-- -->Feb 19, 2026<a href="#stable-3.300-14" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to stable-3.300-14" title="Direct link to stable-3.300-14">​</a></h4><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" contents.</li><li>Fixed an issue where GitLab source control commits failed due to incorrect encoding of commit actions.</li></ul></div></div></details><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>security-fix</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Fixed a security vulnerability in the Mailgun email webhook endpoint that could allow an unauthenticated attacker to exfiltrate the Mailgun API key.</li></ul></div></div></details></div><div><h4 class="anchor anchorWithStickyNavbar_loeA" id="stable-3.300-13">3.300.13 – <!-- --> <!-- -->Feb 18, 2026<a href="#stable-3.300-13" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to stable-3.300-13" title="Direct link to stable-3.300-13">​</a></h4><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>fixed</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Fixed an issue where global error handlers for workflows would trigger even when errors were already handled by block-level <strong>On Error</strong> handlers.</li><li>Fixed an issue where branch syncing incorrectly deleted release artifacts, manifests, and other non-branching files during merge commits.</li><li>Fixed an issue where Azure Repos source control diffs included directory entries as files, which caused deployment errors during partial deploys.</li><li>Fixed an issue with GitHub OAuth for MCP resources by including the required <code>Accept: application/json</code> header in access token requests.</li><li>Fixed an issue where auto catchup commits in source control corrupted binary release artifact zip files by incorrectly reading binary content as UTF-8.</li><li>Fixed an issue where admins were unable to delete or move workflows when <code>VERSION_CONTROL_LOCKED</code> is enabled.</li></ul></div></div></details></div><div><h4 class="anchor anchorWithStickyNavbar_loeA" handling.</li></ul></div></div></details><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>fixed</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Fixed an issue that caused an error when connecting to Snowflake via OAuth. Retool no longer sends the parameter <code>prompt</code>. This extension to the OAuth protocol is not supported by Snowflake, and was ignored in the past, but now Snowflake treats it as an error.</li></ul></div></div></details><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>improved</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Improved accessibility features with keyboard navigation and screen reader support enhancements.</li></ul></div></div></details><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>security-fix</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Added postMessage origin validation for custom component collections to prevent cross-origin security issues.</li><li>Added sanitization for all Databricks connection string inputs to prevent parameter injection attacks.</li></ul></div></div></details></div><div><h4 class="anchor anchorWithStickyNavbar_loeA" id="stable-3.300-2">3.300.2 – <!-- --> <!-- -->Dec 17, 2025<a href="#stable-3.300-2" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to stable-3.300-2" title="Direct link to stable-3.300-2">​</a></h4><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>fixed</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Fixed an issue where the <strong>Re-auth</strong> button did not show for resource query tools in the agents tool creation canvas.</li><li>Fixed an issue where users needed to be admins to have access to source control. Users just need manage access.</li></ul></div></div></details><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>improved</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li></li></ul></div></div></details><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>security-fix</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Changed behavior so that the HTTP path field in the Databricks resource now sanitizes semicolons to prevent JDBC parameter injection. If you were previously including connection parameters in the HTTP path (e.g., <code>/sql/1.0/warehouses/abc;parameter=value</code>), these will now be stripped. Use the dedicated connection parameters field instead.</li></ul></div></div></details></div><div><h4 class="anchor anchorWithStickyNavbar_loeA" id="stable-3.300-1">3.300.1 – <!-- --> <!-- -->Dec 10, multi-instance releases so users can protect an element, create a release artifact, and update the manifest in the same PR.</li><li>Fixed an issue where reset password confirmation emails would still be sent to users even when reset password emails are disabled in an organization.</li></ul></div></div></details><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>added</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Added a feature flag <code>sourceControlConfigAllowTemplates</code> that enables Source Control configurations to use configuration variables and/or Secrets Manager secrets for sensitive credential fields.</li><li>Added support for drag-and-drop page reordering.</li><li>Added a new API endpoint, Get IP Allowlist By Region, which returns Retool&#x27;s whitelisted IP addresses.</li><li>Added audit log events for Source Control deployments.</li><li>Added support for managed key AI features when using a HTTP proxy.</li><li>Added permission checks for page cloning.</li><li>Added options to select either Amazon Bedrock, OpenAI, or Anthropic as the single-model provider for Assist.</li><li>Added support for Claude Haiku 4.5.</li><li>Added support for README interactions to Assist.</li><li>Added the <code>RESOURCE_TYPES_DENY_LIST</code> environment variable to prevent users from creating and running against the provided resource types.</li><li>Added support to Assist for referencing global objects in Javascript queries and transformers.</li><li>Added automatic app name generation to empty apps when using Assist.</li><li>Added the <code>RTEL_SEND_TO_RETOOL_INPUT_ALLOWLIST</code> environment variable to specify which data to send to Retool&#x27;s telemetry server.</li><li>Added a call to action in all single-page apps that prompts users to migrate to multipage.</li><li>Added support for multiple configurations in Secrets Manager.</li><li>Added web grounding support for Google Gemini models, allowing them to search the web for up-to-date information when answering queries.</li><li>Added new beta features for Secrets Manager in on-premise instances, allowing multiple Secrets Manager configurations to be used at once (to get secrets from different providers, or from different areas within the same provider).</li><li>Added a CTA to the homepage announcing Assist.</li><li>Added an option to exclude Table columns from search.</li><li>Added <code>cmd+i</code> as a new keyboard shortcut to toggle the Assist panel open or closed.</li><li>Added toggling the properties.</li><li>Added more detailed response messages for insufficient user permissions when editing Agents.</li><li>Added an empty object default for the <code>GET /resource_configurations</code> flickering when scrolling through a group&#x27;s members list.</li><li>Fixed an issue that prevented a tool from appearing in the UI during agent execution if the tool had a long description (&gt;2000 If a single action in a menu is disabled, a tooltip is added upon hover.</li><li>Changed the behavior when a user tries to access a Workflow they don&#x27;t have permissions for. Now they will be redirected back to the workflows landing page with an error toast.</li><li>Changed all emails from Retool so that they use the most updated Retool logo.</li><li>Changed behavior so that if the <code>snowflakeShowPopulateQueryTagOption</code> feature flag is set, the Snowflake resource options now include &quot;Automatically set QUERY_TAG on all queries&quot;. Checking this box makes Retool generate a <code>QUERY_TAG</code> for every query to that resource, whose value is a JSON object with information about the resource and the source of the query.</li><li>OAuth resources are now only available when using directly invoked workflows, apps, and agent tool calls.</li><li>Changed apps to use a default width of <code>100%</code>. This reverts a previous change that made apps <code>1200px</code> wide by default.</li><li>Changed workflow overage emails so that they include the organization subdomain.</li><li>Changed Kafka, SQS, SNS, and Tavily Web Search integrations from beta to general availability.</li><li>Changed the login page text content.</li><li>Updated the menu options for blocks in workflow functions.</li><li>Moved the <strong>Close</strong> button for workflow functions to the top right.</li><li>Changed a rule so that non-admins (with proper role) can provide tokens to create custom components.</li><li>Changed per-screen permissions to be enabled by default for Enterprise customers.</li></ul></div></div></details><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>deprecated</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Deprecated the open source <code>llama-4-maverick</code> AI model in favor of <code>kimi-k2-instruct-0905</code>.</li><li>Deprecated the <code>llama-4</code> model in the open source AI provider. This has been replaced with <code>kimi-k2-instruct-0905</code>.</li><li>Deprecated OpenAI&#x27;s GPT-3.5-turbo-instruct model in favor of GPT-4.0-mini.</li><li>Deprecated Claude 3.5 Sonnet in favor of Claude Sonnet 4.5.</li></ul></div></div></details></div></section><section class="margin-vert--lg"><h2 class="anchor anchorWithStickyNavbar_loeA" id="3.284">Self-hosted Retool 3.284<a href="#3.284" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Self-hosted Retool 3.284" title="Direct link to Self-hosted Retool 3.284">​</a></h2><p><span class="badge badge--warning">No longer supported</span></p><table class="margin-bottom--lg"><tbody><tr><td>First release version</td><td>3.284<!-- -->.<!-- -->0</td><td>October 21, 2025</td><td><a href="https://hub.docker.com/r/tryretool/backend/tags?name=3.284.0" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">tryretool/backend:<!-- -->3.284<!-- -->.<!-- -->0<!-- -->-stable on Dockerhub</a></td></tr><tr><td>Latest release version</td><td>3.284<!-- -->.<!-- -->22</td><td>February 25, 2026</td><td><a href="https://hub.docker.com/r/tryretool/backend/tags?name=3.284.22" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">tryretool/backend:<!-- -->3.284<!-- -->.<!-- -->22<!-- -->-stable on Dockerhub</a></td></tr></tbody></table><h3>Major changes in this release</h3><ul><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/assist" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Assist is now available.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/readme" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Improvements to the README feature of Retool apps are now available.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/agents-source-control" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Agents can now be protected with Source Control.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/branch-merging" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Merging changes from your default branch into your feature branch is now supported in Source Control.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/multi-instance-releases" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Source Control multi-instance releases are now supported.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/databricks-lakebase-integration" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Databricks Lakehouse integration is now available.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/oauth-mcp-agents" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">OAuth support for MCP agents is now available.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/roles-permissions" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Granular admin permissions using role-based access control is now in beta.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/i18n" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Internationalization (i18n) support is now generally available.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/performance-monitoring" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Performance monitoring features have been introduced.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/fullstory-ga" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">FullStory integration is now generally available.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/invoke-agent-block" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">You can now see the output of an agent run with the Result (sync) return type when using the Invoke Agent block in workflows.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/jdbc-removal" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Retool removed some JDBC connectors that were inadvertently included in certain self-hosted release versions.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/custom-component-support-update" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Retool updated the custom component support library to version 1.9.0, which adds a new verbose option with `deploy` and `sync` commands.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/draft-app-permissions" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">You can now restrict users from creating draft apps.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/updated-permissions-for-all-users" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Update to default user permissions on Business and Enterprise plans.</a></li></ul><h3>Patch release notes</h3><div><h4 class="anchor anchorWithStickyNavbar_loeA" id="stable-3.284-22">3.284.22 – <!-- --> <!-- -->Feb 25, 2026<a href="#stable-3.284-22" threads.</li><li>Improved the consistency with which Assist is able to correctly populate the options of a Select input.</li><li>Improved the display of status text in Assist.</li><li>Fixed an issue where Assist would unnecessarily disable row selection on Table components.</li><li>Improved accessibility experience for two-factor authetnication setup.</li></ul></div></div></details><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>changed</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Changed the default permissions for <strong>All users</strong> when creating a new organization on the Business or Enterprise plans. This group now has no permissions by default and can be updated as needed. This does not affect existing organizations.</li><li>Parent window communication in embedded apps is now generally available, and configuring a setting is no longer required.</li><li>Changed the internationalization feature to general availability.</li><li>Changed permission configuration so that users who do not have permission for an agent, regardless of whether or not they have permission for a workflow, will be unable to see the <strong>Agents</strong> tab in the navigation bar.</li><li>Changed the default app width to be 1200px wide.</li><li>Changed apps to use a default width of <code>100%</code>. This reverts a previous change that made apps <code>1200px</code> wide by default.</li></ul></div></div></details><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>removed</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Remove <strong>Last Actions</strong> from Assist Tool Call header.</li></ul></div></div></details><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>deprecated</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Deprecated Gemini 1.5 models. Gemini 2.0 Flash will be used instead.</li></ul></div></div></details></div></section><section class="margin-vert--lg"><h2 class="anchor anchorWithStickyNavbar_loeA" id="3.253">Self-hosted Retool 3.253<a href="#3.253" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Self-hosted Retool 3.253" title="Direct link to Self-hosted Retool 3.253">​</a></h2><p><span class="badge badge--warning">No longer supported</span></p><table class="margin-bottom--lg"><tbody><tr><td>First release version</td><td>3.253<!-- -->.<!-- -->0</td><td>September 09, 2025</td><td><a href="https://hub.docker.com/r/tryretool/backend/tags?name=3.253.0" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">tryretool/backend:<!-- -->3.253<!-- -->.<!-- -->0<!-- -->-stable on Dockerhub</a></td></tr><tr><td>Latest release version</td><td>3.253<!-- -->.<!-- -->28</td><td>February 25, 2026</td><td><a href="https://hub.docker.com/r/tryretool/backend/tags?name=3.253.28" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">tryretool/backend:<!-- -->3.253<!-- -->.<!-- -->28<!-- -->-stable on Dockerhub</a></td></tr></tbody></table><h3>Major changes in this release</h3><ul><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/code-executor-required" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Code executor changes in self-hosted 3.251 and later require updating existing installations.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/bitbucket-access-tokens" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Bitbucket access token support has been added.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/protected-workflow-releases" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">You can now protect workflow releases with Source Control.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/workflow-release-language" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Some terminology changes in the Workflows IDE.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/access-list" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">You can now view which users and permission groups have access to a workflow, resource, and agent.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/module-input-types" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Modules now support typed data inputs. This change makes your modules more reliable by catching mismatched data types early.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/per-page-permissions" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Organizations on the Business or Enterprise plan can now restrict users from accessing specific app pages with per-page permissions.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/uuid-source-control" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Source Control now uses UUIDs to identify protected objects.</a></li><li><a href="https://docs.retool.com/changelog/module-layout" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Modules now have configurable height and overflow options.</a></li></ul><h3>Patch release notes</h3><div><h4 class="anchor anchorWithStickyNavbar_loeA" id="stable-3.253-28">3.253.28 – <!-- --> <!-- -->Feb 25, 2026<a href="#stable-3.253-28" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to stable-3.253-28" title="Direct link to stable-3.253-28">​</a></h4><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>changed</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Changed required permission level for folder delete, rename, and move to trash operations from <code>edit</code> to <code>own</code> access.</li></ul></div></div></details><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>security-fix</summary><div><div folders.</li></ul></div></div></details></div><div><h4 class="anchor anchorWithStickyNavbar_loeA" id="stable-3.253-27">3.253.27 – <!-- --> <!-- -->Feb 18, 2026<a href="#stable-3.253-27" partial deploys.</li><li>Fixed an issue where admins were unable to delete or move workflows when <code>VERSION_CONTROL_LOCKED</code> is enabled.</li><li>Fixed an issue with the source control manifest UI not correctly navigating to directory contents.</li></ul></div></div></details><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" Retool no longer sends the parameter <code>prompt</code>. This extension to the OAuth protocol is not supported by Snowflake, and was ignored in the past, but now Snowflake treats it as an error.</li></ul></div></div></details></div><div><h4 class="anchor anchorWithStickyNavbar_loeA" id="stable-3.253-18">3.253.18 – <!-- --> <!-- -->Dec 18, 2025<a href="#stable-3.253-18" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to stable-3.253-18" title="Direct link to stable-3.253-18">​</a></h4><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>security-fix</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Changed behavior so that the HTTP path field in the Databricks resource now sanitizes semicolons to prevent JDBC parameter injection. If you were previously including connection parameters in the HTTP path (e.g., <code>/sql/1.0/warehouses/abc;parameter=value</code>), these will now be stripped. Use the dedicated connection parameters field instead.</li></ul></div></div></details></div><div><h4 class="anchor anchorWithStickyNavbar_loeA" id="stable-3.253-17">3.253.17 – <!-- --> <!-- -->Dec 11, anchorWithStickyNavbar_loeA" id="stable-3.253-0">3.253.0 – <!-- --> <!-- -->Sep 9, 2025<a href="#stable-3.253-0" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to stable-3.253-0" title="Direct link to stable-3.253-0">​</a></h4><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>added</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Added support for Gemini 2.5 Flash stable model.</li><li>Added streaming support for the self-hosted managed key proxy.</li><li>Added support for AWS Secrets Manager integration to use EKS Pod Identity Associations for authentication.</li><li>Added Retool AI to role permissions.</li><li>Added support for OpenAI&#x27;s <strong>gpt-image-1</strong> model for image generation.</li><li>Added OAuth 2.0 authentication support for the <strong>Databricks</strong> resource. Previously, this option was only available to certain organizations.</li><li>Added <code>nowIndicator</code> support to the <strong>Calendar</strong> component.</li><li>Added <code>DBCONNECTOR_GUI_MODE_POOL_MIN_SIZE</code> and <code>DBCONNECTOR_GUI_MODE_POOL_MAX_SIZE</code> environment variables for tuning database connection behavior for GUI mode queries.</li><li>Added header background and text colors as column properties for the Table component.</li><li>Added audit log coverage for permission changes to apps and workflows for a permission group.</li><li>Added audit log coverage for permission changes to folders and resource folders for a permission group.</li><li>Added audit log coverage for changes to universal access levels on objects and for additional permission updates.</li><li>Added audit log coverage for changes in the folder locations of resources and workflows.</li><li>Added page number UI to the <strong>PDF viewer</strong> component.</li><li>Added an affordance for suppressing page navigation during <strong>app testing</strong> recording.</li><li>Added the <code>operation&#x27;</code>attribute to Datadog performance traces.</li><li>Added the <code>appUuid</code> and <code>traceType</code> tags to all performance monitoring spans.</li><li>Added support for creating an app and release in the same deployment for multi-instance releases beta users.</li><li>Added an option to send email replies directly using SMTP and default Retool Email resources.</li><li>Added <code>access_level</code> to the list of properties returned by the <code>Get user apps and folders</code> user action resource query.</li><li>Added an icon next to certain app releases indicating that they are managed via source control.</li><li>Added the ability to toggle between <strong>JSON</strong> and <strong>Table</strong> formats when viewing query results.</li><li>Added support for <strong>AWS IAM Auth</strong> to authenticate with Retool&#x27;s primary application database.</li><li>Added <strong>Include &quot;Sent via Retool Email&quot; signature</strong> checkbox to Retool Email queries. For Free and Team organizations, this is always checked. For Business and Enterprise organizations, unchecking removes the signature.</li><li>Added GUI Mode to the <strong>Agent Resource Query</strong> for easier invoking and progress checking of agent runs from workflows and apps when not using the Agent Chat component.</li><li>Added resource name filtering for audit logs.</li><li>Added audit log links in app and query menus.</li><li>Added <code>idpProvisioned</code> field to audit log metadata.</li><li>Added a security measure that prevents HTTP-based resources from accessing localhost, unless bypassed via either the <code>ALLOW_PUBLIC_API_LOCAL_HTTP_REQUESTS</code> or <code>ALLOW_LESS_SECURE_LOCAL_HTTP_REQUESTS</code> environment variable.</li><li>Added <code>AGENTS_ENABLED</code> environment variable.</li><li>Added <code>USAGE_API_TOKEN_FILE</code> to the list of environment variables that can be loaded from the file system with <code>RETOOL_LOAD_FILE_SECRETS</code>.</li><li>Added API and UI support for access lists for resources, workflows, and agents.</li><li>Added support for Databricks Lakebase connector, which allows connections to Databricks Lakebase instances using a PostgreSQL protocol.</li><li>Added OAuth 2.0 authentication support for Databricks Lakebase connectors.</li><li>Added a <code>host</code> configuration option for Snowflake proxy connections.</li><li>Added a visual indicator (dashed line) to the Table component&#x27;s column headers with tooltips.</li><li>Added support for wrapping column header text to the Table component.</li><li>Added token-based authentication as an option for Bitbucket repositories.</li><li>Added a <strong>Trash</strong> folder display in the workflows UI with move to trash functionality.</li><li>Added special footer for emails sent by Agents.</li><li>Added ability for admin users to delete elements (apps, workflows, resources, queries, themes) when Source Control is on.</li><li>Added UI changes to allow admin users to delete elements even when <code>VERSION_CONTROL_LOCKED</code> is set to true.</li><li>Added support for using API tokens from parent admin organizations to create external users.</li><li>Added a banner when the workflow doesn&#x27;t include a response block.</li><li>Added a <strong>Modules</strong> tab to the <strong>Add component</strong> popover.</li></ul></div></div></details><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>fixed</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Fixed an issue where disabled options in the show after switching pages.</li><li>Fixed an issue where custom CSS was not preserved when converting an app to multipage.</li><li>Fixed an issue with text overflow for property values and parameters.</li><li>Fixed an issue where Select components would not display the option list correctly on mobile browsers.</li><li>Fixed an issue where the license status was not always checked when streaming functionality to fail.</li><li>Fixed an issue where icons were not displaying properly.</li><li>Fixed an issue where <strong>Table</strong> column option lists would not properly update if they reference <code>currentRow</code> or <code>currentSourceRow</code>.</li><li>Fixed an issue where Retool would display a &quot;Validation error&quot; when a user logged in with SSO OIDC and endpoints.</li><li>Improved execution of workflows with the &#x27;function&#x27; triggerType.</li><li>Improved descriptions for migration commits for better clarity.</li><li>Improved the navigation to selected table when clicking on Retool DB resource link in Forms editor.</li><li>Improved resizing support on the source control deployments page.</li><li>Improved the radio button for permission group selection for consistent UI experience across access type selectors.</li><li>Improved the OpenAPI resource integration to support text responses similar to REST API resources.</li><li>Select and Radio Group components now support label wrapping.</li><li>Improved component documentation links to component guides instead of component references where available.</li><li>Improved overflow handling for long email addresses in usage analytics <strong>Top viewers</strong> list.</li><li>Improved API documentation by correcting the Retool version information for access lists with types resources, workflows, and agents.</li><li>Improved performance for multipage apps by optimizing dependency graph calculations.</li></ul></div></div></details><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>changed</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Changed workflow permissions to now require owner permissions.</li><li>Changed &quot;Preview&quot; button text to &quot;Test&quot;.</li><li>Changed access restrictions for public apps in use by organizations that downgraded.</li><li>Removed VM2 dependency. Running workflows and Firebase <strong>Raw mode</strong> queries now require the <strong>Code Executor</strong> service to be deployed to work properly.</li><li>Changed the default access permission when creating Google Sheets resources to read only.</li><li>Upgraded CircleCI API dependencies.</li><li>Changed SQL editor behavior by removing ambiguous preview functionality to prevent accidental query execution.</li><li>Removed <strong>GUI Mode</strong> from the <strong>Agent Resource Query</strong> configuration.</li><li>Changed public app creation to require verified email addresses.</li><li>Updated Retool API to use the  <strong>OpenAPI 3.0.4</strong> spec.</li><li>Changed MySQL resources to use the improved MySQL Connector by default. Changed Databricks resources to consistently use the Java DB connector for better performance and reliability. V1 Connectors for MySQL and Databricks are deprecated and cannot be used anymore.</li></ul></div></div></details><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" components.</li><li>Added a hover tooltip for some instances of truncated text in style editors.</li><li>Added the ability to undo and redo changes in the theme editor with keyboard shortcuts.</li><li>Added support for localizing public apps.</li><li>Added the ability for multipage users to add page-scoped keyboard shortcuts. These override globally-scoped <a href="https://docs.retool.com/apps/reference/keyboard-shortcuts">custom keyboard shortcuts</a>.</li><li>Added border-radius style property to Listbox component.</li><li>Added an error message to indicate rate limiting for custom components.</li><li>Added support for multi-instance releases. This feature is in beta and can be enabled from the Settings &gt; Beta page. Contact Support if you`d like to be added to the Beta.</li><li>Added support for viewing and deleting registered push notification applications from <strong>Mobile Advanced Settings</strong>.</li><li>Added a new editor option that controls whether the label text of a Button wraps (default behavior) or truncates (new option).</li><li>Added support for localizing components into 7 languages (Enterprise plans only).</li><li>Added metadata to the &quot;User invited&quot; Retool Event.</li><li>Added support for comma separators in the Statistics component, formatted based on the browser`s locale settings.</li><li>Added the ability to rename a query by double-clicking the query title.</li><li>Add the <code>api/v2/source_control/test_deploy</code> endpoint to Retool API.</li><li>Added style options for the Table component`s summary row.</li><li>Added support for custom headers in the custom component CLI.</li><li>Added support for viewing and deleting registered push notification applications from <strong>Mobile Advanced Settings</strong>.</li><li>Added the <strong>Restore generated color</strong> option for <strong>Primary border</strong> and <strong>Secondary border</strong> in the theme editor.</li><li>Added a confirmation modal when deleting a theme.</li><li>Added support for <strong>Click</strong> event handlers to the Avatar component.</li><li>Added shadow styles for components and new shadow theme properties.</li><li>Added an error message that indicates failed manifest fetching to the <strong>Settings</strong> page.</li><li>Added undo/redo keyboard shortcut functionality for the theme editor.</li><li>Added support for multi-step workflows in public beta on self-hosted organizations.</li></ul></div></div></details><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>fixed</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Fixed an issue where dragging the pop-out editor for style editors would not work.</li><li>Fixes a regression where modules in &quot;expand to fit&quot; containers would not scroll.</li><li>Fixed an issue where JIT-provisioned users were not added to the <strong>External Users</strong> group.</li><li>Fixed an issue with container borders where they covered small shadows.</li><li>Fixed the module tutorial close button, which was previously invisible.</li><li>Fixed an issue with FIDO2 authentication redirects.</li><li>Fixed focus state and layout shift for multiline contents in style editors.</li><li>Fixed the MySQL connector version 2.0 to support variable assignment.</li><li>Fixed an issue where margin and padding properties were not searchable in the Code search tab.</li><li>Fixed an issue with loading the mobile app editor while having the <code>SANDBOX_DOMAIN</code> environment variable set.</li><li>Fixed an issue with the Chat component not permanently removing message history.</li><li>Fixed an issue with the Chat component so that the empty state is centered when the message goes to multiple lines.</li><li>Fixed a bug that would cause issues with virtualization of dropdown items in a Select component when using a larger font size.</li><li>Fixed an issue causing a redirect loop for 2FA-enabled logins.</li><li>Fixed a bug that caused child items of disabled vertical Navigation components to be clickable when they should be disabled.</li><li>Fixed a small visual regression on Checkboxes created on versions before 3.75.0.</li><li>Fixed the Table toolbar grouping menu, which showed a blank input after using the <code>setGrouping</code> method.</li><li>Fixed an issue with Source Control where pull request preview links did not correctly reflect subfolder organization.</li><li>Fixed an issue where dynamic expressions could not be used in number-formatted property inputs.</li><li>Fixed an issue with OAuth callbacks and Source Control.</li><li>Fixed an issue where clearing a Form containing a Rich Text Editor would result in the string &quot;null&quot; being set as the value of the component.</li><li>Fixed an issue where component names prevented editing the component.</li><li>Fixed alignment of icons in the app editor.</li><li>Fixed a reset branch error when using Toolscript with Source Control.</li><li>Fixed an issue where overwritten Retool Storage files could not have their public access changed.</li><li>Fixed an issue with the theme editor where unsaved edits were discarded if the theme was renamed.</li><li>Fixed an issue with custom components where new state properties weren`t properly
recognized until a full page refresh.</li><li>Fix an issue with query inputs in the Query Library.</li><li>Fixed an issue where the Checkbox Tree component would render without a tree layout until a user interacts with it.</li><li>Fixed an issue where the Table component stops responding when editing a Tag or Tags column after using <code>setSort()</code>.</li><li>Fixed an issue with the theme editor when referencing user colors.</li><li>Fixed an issue where the Styles editor would disappear when repositioned.</li><li>Fixed an issue with two-factor authentication redirects for FIDO2 users.</li><li>Fixed an issue where Navigation component event handlers were disappearing when added as children to other events.</li></ul></div></div></details><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>improved</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Improved the default settings for the Stacks component.</li><li>Improved the number of unnecessary query runs connected to Table pagination.</li><li>Improved appearance of segmented controls in the Inspector.</li><li>Improved the file upload error message in Retool Storage to include the maximum file size if the limit is exceeded.</li><li>Updated color inputs in the new Chart components to include
color tokens from the theme.</li><li>Clarifies disabled tooltip for the &quot;Upgrade components&quot; menu item.</li><li>Improved the appearance of theme settings when there are no custom themes.</li><li>Improved error messaging if the environment variable <code>SANDBOX_DOMAIN</code> is set to an invalid URL.</li><li>Improved handling of circular dependencies in the theme editor.</li></ul></div></div></details><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>changed</summary><div><div component now prevents <strong>Click row</strong> event handler actions.</li><li>Changed app creation options to create multipage apps by default.</li><li>File input components now include Retool Storage queries.</li><li>Summary rows and number aggregation functions in the Table component now ignore <code>null</code> and <code>undefined</code> values.</li><li>Changed the appearance of font href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Quirks_Mode_and_Standards_Mode">no-quirks mode</a>. This may cause some custom components to render differently when upgrading to 3.52. Starred items now appear at the top of the list.</li><li>Removed the password protection option from publicly accessible apps.</li></ul></div></div></details></div></section><section class="margin-vert--lg"><h2 class="anchor anchorWithStickyNavbar_loeA" id="3.33">Self-hosted Retool 3.33<a href="#3.33" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Self-hosted Retool 3.33" stable-3.33-1">​</a></h4><details class="details_lb9f alert alert--secondary details_r1OI" data-collapsed="true"><summary>improved</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul><li>Added a Retool API endpoint for <code>getResourceById</code>.</li><li>Added style properties for the <strong>Top Bar</strong> icon in the IFrame component.</li><li>Added a <strong>Checked Border</strong> style property to Switch, Checkbox, and Radio Group components.</li><li>Added the Grayscale style option to the Image component.</li><li>Added the Button Group component.</li><li>Added active and hover link style properties for Link, Toggle Link, and Link List components.</li><li>Added visibility of Hover Background color style properties for the Tabs component.</li><li>Added the option to use Automatic colors for the Avatar Group component background color.</li><li>Added the HTML component.</li><li>Added a warning message when attempting to use translation tools to translate the content of Retool apps.</li><li>Added support to configure workflow limits or turn off monitoring entirely when running workflows without code executor.</li><li>Added support for Google service accounts to the REST API resource.</li><li>Added support for dynamically setting the <code>requireConfirmation</code> property of queries.</li><li>Added support for Source Control settings to audit logs.</li><li>Added the new List View component.</li><li>Added dependency cycle error messages to the debugging console.</li><li>Added support for setting the border radius style for Button components.</li><li>Added the option to reset an app theme.</li><li>Added a warning when using a page translation tool that it may not function as expected.</li><li>Added helper methods on <code>_tool</code>.</li><li>Added support for multiple environments to Retool Storage.</li><li>Added support for custom widths to the Drawer frame.</li><li>Added the option to control universal access to the All Users permissions group.</li><li>Added the option to configure security content in <strong>Advanced</strong> settings.</li><li>Added the option to rename app frames from the canvas in the App IDE.</li><li>Added the option to export an app as JSON, with existing query data, in the debugging tools.</li><li>Added frames to be viewed in the State tab.</li><li>Added query payload size to the <strong>Lint</strong> tab of the debugging tools.</li><li>Added the option to expand grouped rows by default in the Table component.</li><li>Added the new Key Value component.</li><li>Expose the <code>instanceView</code> scope within repeatable view components.</li><li>Added an escape handler for frames.</li><li>Added a global helper function for swapping items in an array.</li><li>Added <code>LDAP_SERVER_CERTIFICATE</code> and <code>LDAP_SERVER_KEY</code> to the list of all secret environment variables that can be loaded from the file system with <code>RETOOL_LOAD_FILE_SECRETS</code>.</li><li>Added expandable table rows rerpesentation in Toolscript.</li><li>Added keyboard navigation to the Table component summary row.</li><li>Added support for Google Cloud Provider Secrets Manager.</li><li>Added padding controls to Drawer and Modal frames.</li><li>Added a <strong>GUI Mode</strong> toggle to Firebase queries.</li><li>Added a color option to label captions.</li><li>Added support for public apps to Retool Storage.</li><li>Add the <strong>Add component</strong> option to the contextual menu of the canvas.</li><li>Added an option to hover over and copy text from cell tooltips in the Table component.</li><li>Added integration with Google Cloud Provider Secrets Manager.</li><li>Added support for configuration variables in custom API authentication.</li><li>Added an option to customize the true and false icons for Table boolean columns</li><li>Added Modal frames to apps.</li><li>Added editable dynamic columns to the Table component.</li><li>Added option to always show row selection checkboxes when a Table component is in multi-row selection mode.</li><li>Minor fixes and improvements.</li><li>Fixed an issue with the IDE where some keyboard shortcuts may not function correctly.</li><li>Fixed an issue with the dynamic query confirmation modal.</li><li>Fixed an issue with the Line variant for the Tabs component.</li><li>Fixed an issue where bulk deletion of apps may not work as expected.</li><li>Fixed an issue with the <code>readOnly</code> property of the Select component.</li><li>Fixed an issue with vertical alignment of the Status component when it is set to a fixed height.</li><li>Fixed an issue with the <strong>Background color</strong> style of the Navigation component.</li><li>Fixed an issue where deleting a resource may not work as expected.</li><li>Fixed an issue with editing cells of a Table component with expandable rows that may result in rendering content in the wrong place.</li><li>Fixed an issue with the Number Input component where the validation message may appear before any user input.</li><li>Fixed an issue that would cause some icons to use an incorrect color.</li><li>Fixed an issue with Date input components where <code>formattedValue</code> did not include timezone formatting.</li><li>Fixed an issue where bulk-deleting apps may not work as expected</li><li>Fixed an issue with the Select component where the <code>readOnly</code> property may not behave as expected.</li><li>Fixed an issue where the Page Input component&#x27;s <code>aria</code> attribute was not set.</li><li>Fixed an issue where the Chart component may stop responding if value labels were not a string or array.</li><li>Fixed an issue where the Chart component may not render correctly when using JSON metadata.</li><li>Fixed an issue with Oauth callback URLs for resource deployments.</li><li>Fixed an issue with Source Control where some apps were not correctly unprotected.</li><li>Fixed an issue where frames within modules may not function correctly.</li><li>Fixed an issue where the background of Table component cells would change color while editing.</li><li>Fixed an issue with the List View component where the height may not appear as expected under certain conditions.</li><li>Fixed an issue where newly created custom app themes don&#x27;t reflect changes until after refresh.</li><li>Fixed an issue where branding headers did not render with a border correctly.</li><li>Fixed an issue where nested containers within a module may not render with a border.</li><li>Fixed an issue where <strong>Changeset</strong> and <strong>Save</strong> actions were not available in Table components with only editable dynamic columns.</li><li>Fixed an issue where the Filter component may not correctly link to a Table component if used within a module.</li><li>Fixed an issue with the Key Value component not respecting saved property order.</li><li>Fixed an issue where the <code>theme</code> global object did not correctly include organization-defined default theme values.</li><li>Fixed an issue with OAuth replacement for redirect to LDP.</li><li>Fixed reset branch diffs in Source Control.</li><li>Fixed an issue where apps may display visual glitches during navigation.</li><li>Fixed an issue where the <strong>Permissions</strong> settings may stop responding.</li><li>Fixed an issue with resource deletion.</li><li>Fixed an issue where signing in from the Retool Mobile app on Android may fail.</li><li>Fixed an issue where branding header borders were missing.</li><li>Fixed an issue with OAuth 2.0 callback URLs.</li><li>Fixed an issue with accent colors for the Phone Number Input component.</li><li>Fixed an issue with the style color editor.</li><li>Fixed an issue where Table component <strong>Changeset</strong> and <strong>Save</strong> actions were not exposed when using editable dynamic columns.</li><li>Fixed an issue with Source Control branch reset.</li><li>Fixed an issue with the App settings menu.</li><li>Fixed an issue where the <strong>Edit</strong> button for resources in the code editor was not always available.</li><li>Fixed an issue where Visual Studio Code for Windows would not save changes.</li><li>Fixed a number of styling issues with the Date and Date Time components.</li><li>Fixed an issue with the Key Value component where dynamic values may not work when using custom formatting.</li><li>Fixed an issue where Excel and Word documents downloaded from S3 resources may be corrupt.</li><li>Fixed an issue where a Container component was unable to use a dynamic value for the <code>showBorder</code> property.</li><li>Fixed an issue where editing cells in nested tables would collapse the parent row.</li><li>Fixed an issue with using theme colors as background colors for frames.</li><li>Fixed an issue with the layout of the Sidebar frame.</li><li>Fixed an issue with the Main frame background when referencing a theme color.</li><li>Fixed an issue where copy and paste actions may not work with the Table component.</li><li>Fixed an issue with view permissions in the resource editor.</li><li>Fixed an issue where a Table component&#x27;s <strong>Click row</strong> event handler may trigger the on header click.</li><li>Fixed an issue where Table&#x27;s <strong>Alternate row color</strong> property would conflict with the <strong>Row color</strong> property.</li><li>Fixed an issue with text overflow in the Command Palette.</li><li>Fixed the height of Select components without a placeholder and when search is disabled.</li><li>Fixed an issue with the Main frame&#x27;s background color when it references a color from the theme.</li><li>Fixed missing users from the <strong>All Users</strong> group.</li><li>Fixed GitHub commit actions in Source Control.</li><li>Fixed the issue where users are prompted to authenticate for duplicate resources</li><li>Fixed an issue with the Key Value component not always respecting saved property order.</li><li>Fixed an issue with mapped options and custom formatting in the Key Value component.</li><li>Fixed an issue where changeset and save actions were not available in tables with only editable dynamic columns.</li><li>Fixed responsiveness of the styles editor when referencing values`.</li><li>Fixed an issue with resetting branches in Source Control.</li><li>Fixed an OAuth replacement issue for redirects to LDP.</li><li>Fixed an issue where <strong>Collapse empty rows</strong> would not work within repeated containers.</li><li>Fixed an issue with components that use <code>ChevronScrollable</code> that caused the component either to not scroll or only scroll by a small amount.</li><li>Fixed positioning of the Modal frame.</li><li>Fixed the resource authentication prompt occasionally not appearing for some users.</li><li>Fixed an issue where commponent names may appear as tabs in the code editor after undoing changes.</li><li>Fixed an issue with app short links.</li><li>Fixed responsiveness of the tyles editor when referencing values.</li><li>Fixed an issue with the ffmpeg library.</li><li>Fixed an issue with app navigation in Source Control.</li><li>Fixed style menu swatches to match parent container nested styles.</li><li>Fixed nested styles with theme references.</li><li>Fixed code editor performance when using nameless resources.</li><li>Fixed a performance issue when typing quickly in a Styles editor.</li><li>Fixed the default height of components when dragged to the canvas.</li><li>Fixed style editor values resetting unexpectedly.</li><li>Fixed an issue where data updates to the Table component in multi-row selection mode would not update <code>selectedSourceRows</code>.</li><li>Fixed an issue with the Table component&#x27;s cell tooltip editor.</li><li>Fixed resource permissions.</li><li>Fixed an issue when resetting a GitLab branch.</li><li>Fixed an issue with the background color of the Main frame when referencing a color from the theme.</li><li>Fixed an issue with the Styles menu color picker where it would fail to respond.</li><li>Fixed text color for frames on themes where the canvas color and primary surface color are highly contrasting.</li><li>Fixed an issue where newline characters were ignored in the Table component&#x27;s Multiline String format.</li><li>Fixed an issue where Excel exports would prepend <code>&#x27;</code> to negative percent values.</li><li>Fixed an issue where autocomplete in a Table component&#x27;s event handlers settings didn&#x27;t include some additional scope.</li><li>Fixed an issue where some empty Table Tag cells would not show a placeholder when editable.</li><li>Fixed an issue where the <strong>Open App</strong> event handler was not aware of custom scope provided by Table or Dropdown Button components.</li><li>Fixed an issue where the Table component&#x27;s search term property was ignored on mount.</li><li>Fixed an issue where checkboxes in expanded rows would not work without a configured primary key.</li><li>Fixed missing URL hash parameters in some instances on protected branches.</li><li>Fixed an error boundary in debug tools caused by switching themes.</li><li>Fix commit timeouts on large apps.</li><li>Fixed issue where config variables were not updated in OAuth settings.</li><li>Fixed an issue where data updates to a Table component in multi-row selection mode would not update <code>selectedSourceRows</code>.</li><li>Fixed an issue where a Table component&#x27;s editable avatar and tags columns would fail to load with lots of option.</li><li>Removed unnecessary headers from API requests.</li><li>Removed user list from api/user response if user does not have access.</li><li>Improve the behavior of the <code>changeset</code> property in the Table component.</li><li>Improved the appearance of all components.</li><li>Improved the performance of the style settings when using dynamic values.</li><li>Improved the appearance and placement of component names on the canvas.</li><li>Improved preview links for app versions to include the current URL hash.</li><li>Improved performance of the Reorderable List component.</li><li>Improved the ability to select and deselect tags in the Table component.</li><li>Improved the appearance of the Status component.</li><li>Improved the performance of web components with input fields.</li><li>Improved the editing of modules to prevent distructive actions.</li><li>Improved deletion of components.</li><li>Improved the appearance of the <strong>Compare Changes</strong> modal.</li><li>Updated the PDF Exporter to use template string editors.</li><li>Improved date parsing to support second-based unix timestamps.</li><li>Updated design of inputs in Theme editor.</li><li>Reduced latency of source control branch deletion endpoint by 80%.</li><li>Moved Legacy components to the end of the component picker in the IDE.</li><li>Added <code>GIT_POLL_INTERVAL_SECONDS</code> to control the interval to poll for new remote commits in Source Control.</li><li>URL query parameters now retain their original sorting and are no longer sorted alphabetically.</li><li>You must now set the <code>ALLOW_SAME_ORIGIN_OPTION</code> <a href="https://docs.retool.com/reference/environment-variables/general">environment variable</a> to <code>true</code> to use IFrames which use the <code>allow-same-origin</code> sandbox flag.</li><li>Upgrade Node version to 18.18.2.</li><li>Disabled <strong>Storage and cookies</strong> option for custom components by default. This can be re-enabled by setting the <code>ALLOW_SAME_ORIGIN_OPTION</code> environment variable.</li><li>Secondary and tertiary colors in the Theme editor can now be empty.</li><li>Exposed <code>theme.borderRadius</code> to apps.</li><li>Changed the Retool Database connection string modal UI.</li></ul></div></div></details></div></section></section></div><div class="col col--3"><aside
